I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
WebAuthn ignores AuthenticationEventPublisher
**Describe the bug**
WebAuthn does not use the configured (global) `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

looks like `NullEventPublisher` is always used (at least thats what you can see in debug).  
ref. https://github.com/spring-projects/spring-security/blob/7.0.0-RC1/config/src/main/java/org/springframework/security/config/annotation/web/configurers/WebAuthnConfigurer.java#L178-L179

**To Reproduce**
* define an `AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean
* authenticate e.g. with username/password
  * `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` published on the configured `AuthenticationEventPublisher`
* authenticate with a passkey
  * `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` published on a `NullEventPublisher` (and swallowed)

**Expected behavior**
WebAuthn should use the configured (global) `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

**Sample**

sample app will be referenced asap:
* run
* log in as user / password
  * event listener fired, see log
```
2025-10-28T07:04:30.267+01:00  INFO 32928 --- [demo] [nio-8080-exec-6] com.example.demo.AuthenticationEvents    : AuthenticationEvents onSuccess: org.springframework.security.authentication.event.AuthenticationSuccessEvent[source=UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken [Principal=org.springframework.security.core.userdetails.User [Username=user, Password=[PROTECTED], Enabled=true, AccountNonExpired=true, CredentialsNonExpired=true, AccountNonLocked=true, Granted Authorities=[ROLE_USER]], Credentials=[PROTECTED], Authenticated=true, Details=WebAuthenticationDetails [RemoteIpAddress=127.0.0.1, SessionId=C36A389B691D34D30439DB46090194E2], Granted Authorities=[ROLE_USER, FactorGrantedAuthority [authority=FACTOR_PASSWORD, issuedAt=2025-10-28T06:04:30.265508800Z]]]]
```
* http://localhost:8080/webauthn/register
  * register a passkey
* log out
* log in using passkey
  * event listener not fired

</pr_description>

    55	/**
    56	 * Configures WebAuthn for Spring Security applications
    57	 *
    58	 * @param <H> the type of builder
    59	 * @author Rob Winch
    60	 * @since 6.4
    61	 */
    62	public class WebAuthnConfigurer<H extends HttpSecurityBuilder<H>>
    63	                extends AbstractHttpConfigurer<WebAuthnConfigurer<H>, H> {
    64	
    65	        private String rpId;
    66	
    67	        private String rpName;

    78	         * The Relying Party id.
    79	         * @param rpId the relying party id
    80	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
    81	         */
    82	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> rpId(String rpId) {
    83	                Assert.hasText(rpId, "rpId be null or empty");
    84	                this.rpId = rpId;
    85	                return this;
    86	        }
    87	
    88	        /**

    93	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> rpName(String rpName) {
    94	                Assert.hasText(rpName, "rpName can't be null or empty");
    95	                this.rpName = rpName;
    96	                return this;
    97	        }

   105	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> allowedOrigins(String... allowedOrigins) {

   157	        @Override
   158	        public void init(H http) {
   159	                ExceptionHandlingConfigurer<H> exceptions = http.getConfigurer(ExceptionHandlingConfigurer.class);
   160	                if (exceptions != null) {
   161	                        AuthenticationEntryPoint entryPoint = new LoginUrlAuthenticationEntryPoint("/login");
   162	                        exceptions.defaultDeniedHandlerForMissingAuthority((ep) -> ep.defaultEntryPoint(entryPoint),
   163	                                        FactorGrantedAuthority.WEBAUTHN_AUTHORITY);
   164	                }
   165	        }
   166	
   167	        @Override
   168	        public void configure(H http) {
   169	                UserDetailsService userDetailsService = getSharedOrBean(http, UserDetailsService.class)
   170	                        .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Missing UserDetailsService Bean"));
   171	                PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntities = getSharedOrBean(http,
   172	                                PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository.class)
   173	                        .orElse(userEntityRepository());
   174	                UserCredentialRepository userCredentials = getSharedOrBean(http, UserCredentialRepository.class)
   175	                        .orElse(userCredentialRepository());
   176	                WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations rpOperations = webAuthnRelyingPartyOperations(userEntities, userCredentials);
   177	                PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository = creationOptionsRepository();
   178	                WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter webAuthnAuthnFilter = new WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter();
   179	                webAuthnAuthnFilter.setAuthenticationManager(
   180	                                new ProviderManager(new WebAuthnAuthenticationProvider(rpOperations, userDetailsService)));
   181	                webAuthnAuthnFilter = postProcess(webAuthnAuthnFilter);
   182	                WebAuthnRegistrationFilter webAuthnRegistrationFilter = new WebAuthnRegistrationFilter(userCredentials,
   183	                                rpOperations);
   184	                webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setDeleteCredentialAuthorizationManager(
   185	                                new CredentialRecordOwnerAuthorizationManager(userCredentials, userEntities));
   186	                PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsFilter creationOptionsFilter = new PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsFilter(
   187	                                rpOperations);
   188	                if (creationOptionsRepository != null) {
   189	                        webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);
   190	                        creationOptionsFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);
   191	                }
   192	                if (this.converter != null) {
   193	                        webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   194	                        creationOptionsFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   195	                }
   196	                http.addFilterBefore(webAuthnAuthnFilter, BasicAuthenticationFilter.class);
   197	                http.addFilterAfter(webAuthnRegistrationFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);
   198	                http.addFilterBefore(creationOptionsFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);
   199	                http.addFilterBefore(new PublicKeyCredentialRequestOptionsFilter(rpOperations), AuthorizationFilter.class);
   200	
   201	                DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter loginPageGeneratingFilter = http
   202	                        .getSharedObject(DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter.class);
   203	                boolean isLoginPageEnabled = loginPageGeneratingFilter != null && loginPageGeneratingFilter.isEnabled();
   204	                if (isLoginPageEnabled) {
   205	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setPasskeysEnabled(true);
   206	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setResolveHeaders((request) -> {
   207	                                CsrfToken csrfToken = (CsrfToken) request.getAttribute(CsrfToken.class.getName());
   208	                                return Map.of(csrfToken.getHeaderName(), csrfToken.getToken());
   209	                        });
   210	                }
   211	
   212	                if (!this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage) {
   213	                        http.addFilterAfter(new DefaultWebAuthnRegistrationPageGeneratingFilter(userEntities, userCredentials),
   214	                                        AuthorizationFilter.class);
   215	                        if (!isLoginPageEnabled) {
   216	                                http.addFilter(DefaultResourcesFilter.css());
   217	                        }
   218	                }
   219	
   220	                if (isLoginPageEnabled || !this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage) {
   221	                        http.addFilter(DefaultResourcesFilter.webauthn());
   222	                }
   223	        }
   224	
   225	        private PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository() {
   226	                if (this.creationOptionsRepository != null) {
   227	                        return this.creationOptionsRepository;
   228	                }
   229	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   230	                return context.getBeanProvider(PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository.class).getIfUnique();
   231	        }
   232	
   233	        private <C> Optional<C> getSharedOrBean(H http, Class<C> type) {
   234	                C shared = http.getSharedObject(type);
   235	                return Optional.ofNullable(shared).or(() -> getBeanOrNull(type));
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        private <T> Optional<T> getBeanOrNull(Class<T> type) {
   239	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   240	                if (context == null) {
   241	                        return Optional.empty();
   242	                }
   243	                try {
   244	                        return Optional.of(context.getBean(type));
   245	                }
   246	                catch (NoSuchBeanDefinitionException ex) {
   247	                        return Optional.empty();
   248	                }
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        private MapUserCredentialRepository userCredentialRepository() {
   252	                return new MapUserCredentialRepository();
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        private PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntityRepository() {
   256	                return new MapPublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository();
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        private WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations webAuthnRelyingPartyOperations(
   260	                        PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntities, UserCredentialRepository userCredentials) {
   261	                Optional<WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations> webauthnOperationsBean = getBeanOrNull(
   262	                                WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations.class);
   263	                String rpName = (this.rpName != null) ? this.rpName : this.rpId;
   264	                return webauthnOperationsBean
   265	                        .orElseGet(() -> new Webauthn4JRelyingPartyOperations(userEntities, userCredentials,
   266	                                        PublicKeyCredentialRpEntity.builder().id(this.rpId).name(rpName).build(), this.allowedOrigins));
   267	        }
   268	
   269	}

    90	        public WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter() {
    91	                super(pathPattern(HttpMethod.POST, "/login/webauthn"));
    92	                setSecurityContextRepository(new HttpSessionSecurityContextRepository());
    93	                setAuthenticationFailureHandler(
    94	                                new AuthenticationEntryPointFailureHandler(new HttpStatusEntryPoint(HttpStatus.UNAUTHORIZED)));
    95	                setAuthenticationSuccessHandler(new HttpMessageConverterAuthenticationSuccessHandler());

    98	        @Override
    99	        public Authentication attemptAuthentication(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response)
   100	                        throws AuthenticationException, IOException, ServletException {
   101	                ServletServerHttpRequest httpRequest = new ServletServerHttpRequest(request);
   102	                ResolvableType resolvableType = ResolvableType.forClassWithGenerics(PublicKeyCredential.class,
   103	                                AuthenticatorAssertionResponse.class);
   104	                PublicKeyCredential<AuthenticatorAssertionResponse> publicKeyCredential = null;
   105	                try {
   106	                        publicKeyCredential = (PublicKeyCredential<AuthenticatorAssertionResponse>) this.converter
   107	                                .read(resolvableType, httpRequest, null);
   108	                }
   109	                catch (Exception ex) {
   110	                        throw new BadCredentialsException("Unable to authenticate the PublicKeyCredential", ex);
   111	                }
   112	                PublicKeyCredentialRequestOptions requestOptions = this.requestOptionsRepository.load(request);
   113	                if (requestOptions == null) {
   114	                        throw new BadCredentialsException(
   115	                                        "Unable to authenticate the PublicKeyCredential. No PublicKeyCredentialRequestOptions found.");
   116	                }
   117	                this.requestOptionsRepository.save(request, response, null);
   118	                RelyingPartyAuthenticationRequest authenticationRequest = new RelyingPartyAuthenticationRequest(requestOptions,
   119	                                publicKeyCredential);
   120	                WebAuthnAuthenticationRequestToken token = new WebAuthnAuthenticationRequestToken(authenticationRequest);
   121	                return getAuthenticationManager().authenticate(token);
   122	        }
   123

   165	         * @author Rob Winch
   166	         * @since 7.0
   167	         */
   168	        private static final class GenericHttpMessageConverterAdapter<T> extends AbstractSmartHttpMessageConverter<T> {
   169	
   170	                private final GenericHttpMessageConverter<T> delegate;
   171	
   172	                private GenericHttpMessageConverterAdapter(GenericHttpMessageConverter<T> delegate) {
   173	                        Assert.notNull(delegate, "delegate cannot be null");
   174	                        this.delegate = delegate;
   175	                }
   176	
   177	                @Override
   178	                public boolean canRead(ResolvableType type, @Nullable MediaType mediaType) {
   179	                        Class<?> clazz = type.resolve();
   180	                        return (clazz != null) ? canRead(clazz, mediaType) : canRead(mediaType);
   181	                }
   182	
   183	                @Override
   184	                public boolean canRead(Class<?> clazz, @Nullable MediaType mediaType) {
   185	                        return this.delegate.canRead(clazz, mediaType);
   186	                }
   187	
   188	                @Override
   189	                public boolean canWrite(Class<?> clazz, @Nullable MediaType mediaType) {
   190	                        return this.delegate.canWrite(clazz, mediaType);
   191	                }
   192

   195	                        return this.delegate.getSupportedMediaTypes();
   196	                }

   200	                        return this.delegate.getSupportedMediaTypes(clazz);

    51	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.session.NullAuthenticatedSessionStrategy;
    52	import org.springframework.security.web.authentication.session.SessionAuthenticationStrategy;
    53	import org.springframework.security.web.context.RequestAttributeSecurityContextRepository;
    54	import org.springframework.security.web.context.SecurityContextRepository;
    55	import org.springframework.security.web.util.matcher.RequestMatcher;
    56	import org.springframework.util.Assert;
    57	import org.springframework.web.filter.GenericFilterBean;
    58	
    59	import static org.springframework.security.web.servlet.util.matcher.PathPatternRequestMatcher.pathPattern;
    60	
    61	/**
    62	 * Abstract processor of browser-based HTTP-based authentication requests.
    63	 *
    64	 * <h3>Authentication Process</h3>
    65	 *
    66	 * The filter requires that you set the <tt>authenticationManager</tt> property. An
    67	 * <tt>AuthenticationManager</tt> is required to process the authentication request tokens
    68	 * created by implementing classes.
    69	 * <p>
    70	 * This filter will intercept a request and attempt to perform authentication from that
    71	 * request if the request matches the
    72	 * {@link #setRequiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher(RequestMatcher)}.
    73	 * <p>
    74	 * Authentication is performed by the
    75	 * {@link #attemptAuthentication(HttpServletRequest, HttpServletResponse)
    76	 * attemptAuthentication} method, which must be implemented by subclasses.
    77	 *
    78	 * <h4>Authentication Success</h4>
    79	 *
    80	 * If authentication is successful, the resulting {@link Authentication} object will be
    81	 * placed into the <code>SecurityContext</code> for the current thread, which is
    82	 * guaranteed to have already been created by an earlier filter.
    83	 * <p>
    84	 * The configured {@link #setAuthenticationSuccessHandler(AuthenticationSuccessHandler)
    85	 * AuthenticationSuccessHandler} will then be called to take the redirect to the
    86	 * appropriate destination after a successful login. The default behaviour is implemented
    87	 * in a {@link SavedRequestAwareAuthenticationSuccessHandler} which will make use of any
    88	 * <tt>DefaultSavedRequest</tt> set by the <tt>ExceptionTranslationFilter</tt> and
    89	 * redirect the user to the URL contained therein. Otherwise it will redirect to the
    90	 * webapp root "/". You can customize this behaviour by injecting a differently configured
    91	 * instance of this class, or by using a different implementation.
    92	 * <p>
    93	 * See the
    94	 * {@link #successfulAuthentication(HttpServletRequest, HttpServletResponse, FilterChain, Authentication)}
    95	 * method for more information.
    96	 *
    97	 * <h4>Authentication Failure</h4>
    98	 *
    99	 * If authentication fails, it will delegate to the configured
   100	 * {@link AuthenticationFailureHandler} to allow the failure information to be conveyed to
   101	 * the client. The default implementation is {@link SimpleUrlAuthenticationFailureHandler}
   102	 * , which sends a 401 error code to the client. It may also be configured with a failure
   103	 * URL as an alternative. Again you can inject whatever behaviour you require here.
   104	 *
   105	 * <h4>Event Publication</h4>
   106	 *
   107	 * If authentication is successful, an {@link InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent} will
   108	 * be published via the application context. No events will be published if authentication
   109	 * was unsuccessful, because this would generally be recorded via an
   110	 * {@code AuthenticationManager}-specific application event.
   111	 *
   112	 * <h4>Session Authentication</h4>
   113	 *
   114	 * The class has an optional {@link SessionAuthenticationStrategy} which will be invoked
   115	 * immediately after a successful call to {@code attemptAuthentication()}. Different
   116	 * implementations {@link #setSessionAuthenticationStrategy(SessionAuthenticationStrategy)
   117	 * can be injected} to enable things like session-fixation attack prevention or to control
   118	 * the number of simultaneous sessions a principal may have.
   119	 *
   120	 * @author Ben Alex
   121	 * @author Luke Taylor
   122	 */
   123	public abstract class AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter extends GenericFilterBean
   124	                implements ApplicationEventPublisherAware, MessageSourceAware {
   125	
   126	        private SecurityContextHolderStrategy securityContextHolderStrategy = SecurityContextHolder
   127	                .getContextHolderStrategy();
   128	
   129	        protected @Nullable ApplicationEventPublisher eventPublisher;
   130	
   131	        protected AuthenticationDetailsSource<HttpServletRequest, ?> authenticationDetailsSource = new WebAuthenticationDetailsSource();
   132	
   133	        private AuthenticationConverter authenticationConverter = (request) -> {
   134	                throw new AuthenticationCredentialsNotFoundException(
   135	                                "Please either configure an AuthenticationConverter or override attemptAuthentication when extending AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter");
   136	        };
   137	
   138	        @SuppressWarnings("NullAway.Init")
   139	        private AuthenticationManager authenticationManager;
   140	
   141	        protected MessageSourceAccessor messages = SpringSecurityMessageSource.getAccessor();
   142	
   143	        private RememberMeServices rememberMeServices = new NullRememberMeServices();
   144	
   145	        private RequestMatcher requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher;
   146	
   147	        private boolean continueChainBeforeSuccessfulAuthentication = false;
   148	
   149	        private boolean continueChainWhenNoAuthenticationResult;
   150	
   151	        private SessionAuthenticationStrategy sessionStrategy = new NullAuthenticatedSessionStrategy();
   152	
   153	        private boolean allowSessionCreation = true;
   154	
   155	        private AuthenticationSuccessHandler successHandler = new SavedRequestAwareAuthenticationSuccessHandler();
   156	
   157	        private AuthenticationFailureHandler failureHandler = new SimpleUrlAuthenticationFailureHandler();
   158	
   159	        private SecurityContextRepository securityContextRepository = new RequestAttributeSecurityContextRepository();
   160	
   161	        private boolean mfaEnabled;
   162	
   163	        /**
   164	         * @param defaultFilterProcessesUrl the default value for <tt>filterProcessesUrl</tt>.
   165	         */
   166	        protected AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter(String defaultFilterProcessesUrl) {
   167	                this(pathPattern(defaultFilterProcessesUrl));
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        /**
   171	         * Creates a new instance
   172	         * @param requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher the {@link RequestMatcher} used to
   173	         * determine if authentication is required. Cannot be null.
   174	         */
   175	        protected AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter(RequestMatcher requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher) {
   176	                Assert.notNull(requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher, "requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher cannot be null");
   177	                this.requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher = requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher;
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        /**
   181	         * Creates a new instance with a default filterProcessesUrl and an
   182	         * {@link AuthenticationManager}
   183	         * @param defaultFilterProcessesUrl the default value for <tt>filterProcessesUrl</tt>.
   184	         * @param authenticationManager the {@link AuthenticationManager} used to authenticate
   185	         * an {@link Authentication} object. Cannot be null.
   186	         */
   187	        protected AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter(String defaultFilterProcessesUrl,
   188	                        AuthenticationManager authenticationManager) {
   189	                this(pathPattern(defaultFilterProcessesUrl));
   190	                setAuthenticationManager(authenticationManager);
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        /**
   194	         * Creates a new instance with a {@link RequestMatcher} and an
   195	         * {@link AuthenticationManager}
   196	         * @param requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher the {@link RequestMatcher} used to
   197	         * determine if authentication is required. Cannot be null.
   198	         * @param authenticationManager the {@link AuthenticationManager} used to authenticate
   199	         * an {@link Authentication} object. Cannot be null.
   200	         */
   201	        protected AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter(RequestMatcher requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher,
   202	                        AuthenticationManager authenticationManager) {
   203	                setRequiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher(requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher);
   204	                setAuthenticationManager(authenticationManager);
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        @Override
   208	        public void afterPropertiesSet() {
   209	                Assert.notNull(this.authenticationManager, "authenticationManager must be specified");
   210	        }
   211	
   212	        /**
   213	         * Invokes the {@link #requiresAuthentication(HttpServletRequest, HttpServletResponse)
   214	         * requiresAuthentication} method to determine whether the request is for
   215	         * authentication and should be handled by this filter. If it is an authentication
   216	         * request, the {@link #attemptAuthentication(HttpServletRequest, HttpServletResponse)
   217	         * attemptAuthentication} will be invoked to perform the authentication. There are
   218	         * then three possible outcomes:
   219	         * <ol>
   220	         * <li>An <tt>Authentication</tt> object is returned. The configured
   221	         * {@link SessionAuthenticationStrategy} will be invoked (to handle any
   222	         * session-related behaviour such as creating a new session to protect against
   223	         * session-fixation attacks) followed by the invocation of
   224	         * {@link #successfulAuthentication(HttpServletRequest, HttpServletResponse, FilterChain, Authentication)}
   225	         * method</li>
   226	         * <li>An <tt>AuthenticationException</tt> occurs during authentication. The
   227	         * {@link #unsuccessfulAuthentication(HttpServletRequest, HttpServletResponse, AuthenticationException)
   228	         * unsuccessfulAuthentication} method will be invoked</li>
   229	         * <li>Null is returned, indicating that the authentication process is incomplete. The
   230	         * method will then return immediately, assuming that the subclass has done any
   231	         * necessary work (such as redirects) to continue the authentication process. The
   232	         * assumption is that a later request will be received by this method where the
   233	         * returned <tt>Authentication</tt> object is not null.
   234	         * </ol>
   235	         */
   236	        @Override
   237	        public void doFilter(ServletRequest request, ServletResponse response, FilterChain chain)
   238	                        throws IOException, ServletException {
   239	                doFilter((HttpServletRequest) request, (HttpServletResponse) response, chain);
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        private void doFilter(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response, FilterChain chain)
   243	                        throws IOException, ServletException {
   244	                if (!requiresAuthentication(request, response)) {
   245	                        chain.doFilter(request, response);
   246	                        return;
   247	                }
   248	                try {
   249	                        Authentication authenticationResult = attemptAuthentication(request, response);
   250	                        if (authenticationResult == null) {
   251	                                if (this.continueChainWhenNoAuthenticationResult) {
   252	                                        chain.doFilter(request, response);
   253	                                        return;
   254	                                }
   255	                                // return immediately as subclass has indicated that it hasn't completed
   256	                                return;
   257	                        }
   258	                        Authentication current = this.securityContextHolderStrategy.getContext().getAuthentication();
   259	                        if (shouldPerformMfa(current, authenticationResult)) {
   260	                                authenticationResult = authenticationResult.toBuilder()
   261	                                // @formatter:off
   262	                                        .authorities((a) -> {
   263	                                                Set<String> newAuthorities = a.stream()
   264	                                                        .map(GrantedAuthority::getAuthority)
   265	                                                        .collect(Collectors.toUnmodifiableSet());
   266	                                                for (GrantedAuthority currentAuthority : current.getAuthorities()) {
   267	                                                        if (!newAuthorities.contains(currentAuthority.getAuthority())) {
   268	                                                                a.add(currentAuthority);
   269	                                                        }
   270	                                                }
   271	                                        })
   272	                                        .build();
   273	                                        // @formatter:on
   274	                        }
   275	                        this.sessionStrategy.onAuthentication(authenticationResult, request, response);
   276	                        // Authentication success
   277	                        if (this.continueChainBeforeSuccessfulAuthentication) {
   278	                                chain.doFilter(request, response);
   279	                        }
   280	                        successfulAuthentication(request, response, chain, authenticationResult);
   281	                }
   282	                catch (InternalAuthenticationServiceException failed) {
   283	                        this.logger.error("An internal error occurred while trying to authenticate the user.", failed);
   284	                        unsuccessfulAuthentication(request, response, failed);
   285	                }
   286	                catch (AuthenticationException ex) {
   287	                        // Authentication failed
   288	                        unsuccessfulAuthentication(request, response, ex);
   289	                }
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        @Contract("null, _ -> false")
   293	        private boolean shouldPerformMfa(@Nullable Authentication current, Authentication authenticationResult) {
   294	                if (!this.mfaEnabled) {
   295	                        return false;
   296	                }
   297	                if (current == null || !current.isAuthenticated()) {
   298	                        return false;
   299	                }
   300	                if (!declaresToBuilder(authenticationResult)) {
   301	                        return false;
   302	                }
   303	                return current.getName().equals(authenticationResult.getName());
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        private static boolean declaresToBuilder(Authentication authentication) {
   307	                for (Method method : authentication.getClass().getDeclaredMethods()) {
   308	                        if (method.getName().equals("toBuilder") && method.getParameterTypes().length == 0) {
   309	                                return true;
   310	                        }
   311	                }
   312	                return false;
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        /**
   316	         * Indicates whether this filter should attempt to process a login request for the
   317	         * current invocation.
   318	         * <p>
   319	         * It strips any parameters from the "path" section of the request URL (such as the
   320	         * jsessionid parameter in <em>https://host/myapp/index.html;jsessionid=blah</em>)
   321	         * before matching against the <code>filterProcessesUrl</code> property.
   322	         * <p>
   323	         * Subclasses may override for special requirements, such as Tapestry integration.
   324	         * @return <code>true</code> if the filter should attempt authentication,
   325	         * <code>false</code> otherwise.
   326	         */
   327	        protected boolean requiresAuthentication(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) {
   328	                if (this.requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher.matches(request)) {
   329	                        return true;
   330	                }
   331	                if (this.logger.isTraceEnabled()) {
   332	                        this.logger
   333	                                .trace(LogMessage.format("Did not match request to %s", this.requiresAuthenticationRequestMatcher));
   334	                }
   335	                return false;
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        /**
   339	         * Performs actual authentication.
   340	         * <p>
   341	         * The implementation should do one of the following:
   342	         * <ol>
   343	         * <li>Return a populated authentication token for the authenticated user, indicating
   344	         * successful authentication</li>
   345	         * <li>Return null, indicating that the authentication process is still in progress.
   346	         * Before returning, the implementation should perform any additional work required to
   347	         * complete the process.</li>
   348	         * <li>Throw an <tt>AuthenticationException</tt> if the authentication process
   349	         * fails</li>
   350	         * </ol>
   351	         * @param request from which to extract parameters and perform the authentication
   352	         * @param response the response, which may be needed if the implementation has to do a
   353	         * redirect<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

    56	/**
    57	 * Exports the authentication {@link Configuration}
    58	 *
    59	 * @author Rob Winch
    60	 * @author Ngoc Nhan
    61	 * @since 3.2
    62	 *
    63	 */
    64	@Configuration(proxyBeanMethods = false)
    65	@Import(ObjectPostProcessorConfiguration.class)
    66	public class AuthenticationConfiguration {
    67	
    68	        private AtomicBoolean buildingAuthenticationManager = new AtomicBoolean();
    69	
    70	        private ApplicationContext applicationContext;
    71	
    72	        private AuthenticationManager authenticationManager;
    73	
    74	        private boolean authenticationManagerInitialized;
    75	
    76	        private List<GlobalAuthenticationConfigurerAdapter> globalAuthConfigurers = Collections.emptyList();
    77	
    78	        private ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor;
    79	
    80	        @Bean
    81	        public AuthenticationManagerBuilder authenticationManagerBuilder(ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor,
    82	                        ApplicationContext context) {
    83	                LazyPasswordEncoder defaultPasswordEncoder = new LazyPasswordEncoder(context);
    84	                AuthenticationEventPublisher authenticationEventPublisher = getAuthenticationEventPublisher(context);
    85	                DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder result = new DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder(
    86	                                objectPostProcessor, defaultPasswordEncoder);
    87	                if (authenticationEventPublisher != null) {
    88	                        result.authenticationEventPublisher(authenticationEventPublisher);
    89	                }
    90	                return result;
    91	        }
    92	
    93	        @Bean
    94	        public static GlobalAuthenticationConfigurerAdapter enableGlobalAuthenticationAutowiredConfigurer(
    95	                        ApplicationContext context) {
    96	                return new EnableGlobalAuthenticationAutowiredConfigurer(context);
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        @Bean
   100	        public static InitializeUserDetailsBeanManagerConfigurer initializeUserDetailsBeanManagerConfigurer(
   101	                        ApplicationContext context) {
   102	                return new InitializeUserDetailsBeanManagerConfigurer(context);
   103	        }
   104	
   105	        @Bean
   106	        public static InitializeAuthenticationProviderBeanManagerConfigurer initializeAuthenticationProviderBeanManagerConfigurer(
   107	                        ApplicationContext context) {
   108	                return new InitializeAuthenticationProviderBeanManagerConfigurer(context);
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        public AuthenticationManager getAuthenticationManager() {
   112	                if (this.authenticationManagerInitialized) {
   113	                        return this.authenticationManager;
   114	                }
   115	                AuthenticationManagerBuilder authBuilder = this.applicationContext.getBean(AuthenticationManagerBuilder.class);
   116	                if (this.buildingAuthenticationManager.getAndSet(true)) {
   117	                        return new AuthenticationManagerDelegator(authBuilder);
   118	                }
   119	                for (GlobalAuthenticationConfigurerAdapter config : this.globalAuthConfigurers) {
   120	                        authBuilder.apply(config);
   121	                }
   122	                this.authenticationManager = authBuilder.build();
   123	                if (this.authenticationManager == null) {
   124	                        this.authenticationManager = getAuthenticationManagerBean();
   125	                }
   126	                this.authenticationManagerInitialized = true;
   127	                return this.authenticationManager;
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        @Autowired(required = false)
   131	        public void setGlobalAuthenticationConfigurers(List<GlobalAuthenticationConfigurerAdapter> configurers) {
   132	                configurers.sort(AnnotationAwareOrderComparator.INSTANCE);
   133	                this.globalAuthConfigurers = configurers;
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        @Autowired
   137	        public void setApplicationContext(ApplicationContext applicationContext) {
   138	                this.applicationContext = applicationContext;
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        @Autowired
   142	        public void setObjectPostProcessor(ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor) {
   143	                this.objectPostProcessor = objectPostProcessor;
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        private AuthenticationEventPublisher getAuthenticationEventPublisher(ApplicationContext context) {
   147	                if (context.getBeanNamesForType(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class).length > 0) {
   148	                        return context.getBean(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class);
   149	                }
   150	                return this.objectPostProcessor.postProcess(new DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher());
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   154	        private <T> T lazyBean(Class<T> interfaceName) {
   155	                LazyInitTargetSource lazyTargetSource = new LazyInitTargetSource();
   156	                String[] beanNamesForType = BeanFactoryUtils.beanNamesForTypeIncludingAncestors(this.applicationContext,
   157	                                interfaceName);
   158	                if (beanNamesForType.length == 0) {
   159	                        return null;
   160	                }
   161	                String beanName = getBeanName(interfaceName, beanNamesForType);
   162	                lazyTargetSource.setTargetBeanName(beanName);
   163	                lazyTargetSource.setBeanFactory(this.applicationContext);
   164	                ProxyFactoryBean proxyFactory = new ProxyFactoryBean();
   165	                proxyFactory = this.objectPostProcessor.postProcess(proxyFactory);
   166	                proxyFactory.setTargetSource(lazyTargetSource);
   167	                return (T) proxyFactory.getObject();
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        private <T> String getBeanName(Class<T> interfaceName, String[] beanNamesForType) {
   171	                if (beanNamesForType.length == 1) {
   172	                        return beanNamesForType[0];
   173	                }
   174	                List<String> primaryBeanNames = getPrimaryBeanNames(beanNamesForType);
   175	                Assert.isTrue(primaryBeanNames.size() != 0, () -> "Found " + beanNamesForType.length + " beans for type "
   176	                                + interfaceName + ", but none marked as primary");
   177	                Assert.isTrue(primaryBeanNames.size() == 1,
   178	                                () -> "Found " + primaryBeanNames.size() + " beans for type " + interfaceName + " marked as primary");
   179	                return primaryBeanNames.get(0);
   180	        }
   181	
   182	        private List<String> getPrimaryBeanNames(String[] beanNamesForType) {
   183	                List<String> list = new ArrayList<>();
   184	                if (!(this.applicationContext instanceof ConfigurableApplicationContext)) {
   185	                        return Collections.emptyList();
   186	                }
   187	                for (String beanName : beanNamesForType) {
   188	                        if (((ConfigurableApplicationContext) this.applicationContext).getBeanFactory()
   189	                                .getBeanDefinition(beanName)
   190	                                .isPrimary()) {
   191	                                list.add(beanName);
   192	                        }
   193	                }
   194	                return list;
   195	        }
   196	
   197	        private AuthenticationManager getAuthenticationManagerBean() {
   198	                return lazyBean(AuthenticationManager.class);
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        private static class EnableGlobalAuthenticationAutowiredConfigurer extends GlobalAuthenticationConfigurerAdapter {
   202	
   203	                private final ApplicationContext context;
   204	
   205	                private static final Log logger = LogFactory.getLog(EnableGlobalAuthenticationAutowiredConfigurer.class);
   206	
   207	                EnableGlobalAuthenticationAutowiredConfigurer(ApplicationContext context) {
   208	                        this.context = context;
   209	                }
   210	
   211	                @Override
   212	                public void init(AuthenticationManagerBuilder auth) {
   213	                        Map<String, Object> beansWithAnnotation = this.context
   214	                                .getBeansWithAnnotation(EnableGlobalAuthentication.class);
   215	                        if (logger.isTraceEnabled()) {
   216	                                logger.trace(LogMessage.format("Eagerly initializing %s", beansWithAnnotation));
   217	                        }
   218	                }
   219	
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        /**
   223	         * Prevents infinite recursion in the event that initializing the
   224	         * AuthenticationManager.
   225	         *
   226	         * @author Rob Winch
   227	         * @since 4.1.1
   228	         */
   229	        static final class AuthenticationManagerDelegator implements AuthenticationManager {
   230	
   231	                private AuthenticationManagerBuilder delegateBuilder;
   232	
   233	                private AuthenticationManager delegate;
   234	
   235	                private final Object delegateMonitor = new Object();
   236	
   237	                AuthenticationManagerDelegator(AuthenticationManagerBuilder delegateBuilder) {
   238	                        Assert.notNull(delegateBuilder, "delegateBuilder cannot be null");
   239	                        this.delegateBuilder = delegateBuilder;
   240	                }
   241	
   242	                @Override
   243	                public Authentication authenticate(Authentication authentication) throws AuthenticationException {
   244	                        if (this.delegate != null) {
   245	                                return this.delegate.authenticate(authentication);
   246	                        }
   247	                        synchronized (this.delegateMonitor) {
   248	                                if (this.delegate == null) {
   249	                                        this.delegate = this.delegateBuilder.getObject();
   250	                                        this.delegateBuilder = null;
   251	                                }
   252	                        }
   253	                        return this.delegate.authenticate(authentication);
   254	                }
   255	
   256	                @Override
   257	                public String toString() {
   258	                        return "AuthenticationManagerDelegator [delegate=" + this.delegate + "]";
   259	                }
   260	
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        static class DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder extends AuthenticationManagerBuilder {
   264	
   265	                private PasswordEncoder defaultPasswordEncoder;
   266	
   267	                /**
   268	                 * Creates a new instance
   269	                 * @param objectPostProcessor the {@link ObjectPostProcessor} instance to use.
   270	                 */
   271	                DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder(ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor,
   272	                                PasswordEncoder defaultPasswordEncoder) {
   273	                        super(objectPostProcessor);
   274	                        this.defaultPasswordEncoder = defaultPasswordEncoder;
   275	                }
   276	
   277	                @Override
   278	                public InMemoryUserDetailsManagerConfigurer<AuthenticationManagerBuilder> inMemoryAuthentication() {
   279	                        return super.inMemoryAuthentication().passwordEncoder(this.defaultPasswordEncoder);
   280	                }
   281	
   282	                @Override
   283	                public JdbcUserDetailsManagerConfigurer<AuthenticationManagerBuilder> jdbcAuthentication() {
   284	                        return super.jdbcAuthentication().passwordEncoder(this.defaultPasswordEncoder);
   285	                }
   286	
   287	                @Override
   288	                public <T extends UserDetailsService> DaoAuthenticationConfigurer<AuthenticationManagerBuilder, T> userDetailsService(
   289	                                T userDetailsService) {
   290	                        return super.userDetailsService(userDetailsService).passwordEncoder(this.defaultPasswordEncoder);
   291	                }
   292	
   293	        }
   294	
   295	        static class LazyPasswordEncoder implements PasswordEncoder {
   296	
   297	                private ApplicationContext applicationContext;
   298	
   299	                private PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder;
   300	
   301	                LazyPasswordEncoder(ApplicationContext applicationContext) {
   302	                        this.applicationContext = applicationContext;
   303	                }
   304	
   305	                @Override
   306	                @Contract("!null -> !null; null -> null")
   307	                public String encode(CharSequence rawPassword) {
   308	                        return getPasswordEncoder().encode(rawPassword);
   309	                }
   310	
   311	                @Override
   312	                public boolean matches(CharSequence rawPassword, String encodedPassword) {
   313	                        return getPasswordEncoder().matches(rawPassword, encodedPassword);
   314	                }
   315	
   316	                @Override
   317	                public boolean upgradeEncoding(String encodedPassword) {
   318	                        return getPasswordEncoder().upgradeEncoding(encodedPassword);
   319	                }
   320	
   321	                private PasswordEncoder getPasswordEncoder() {
   322	                        if (this.passwordEncoder != null) {
   323	                                return this.passwordEncoder;
   324	                        }
   325	                        this.passwordEncoder = this.applicationContext.getBeanProvider(PasswordEncoder.class)
   326	                                .getIfUnique(PasswordEncoderFactories::createDelegatingPasswordEncoder);
   327	                        return this.passwordEncoder;
   328	                }
   329	
   330	                @Override
   331	                public String toString() {
   332	                        return getPasswordEncoder().toString();
   333	                }
   334	
   335	        }
   336	
   337	}

    17	package org.springframework.security.authentication;
    18	
    19	import java.util.Arrays;
    20	import java.util.Collections;
    21	import java.util.List;
    22	
    23	import org.apache.commons.logging.Log;
    24	import org.apache.commons.logging.LogFactory;
    25	import org.jspecify.annotations.Nullable;
    26	
    27	import org.springframework.beans.factory.InitializingBean;
    28	import org.springframework.context.MessageSource;
    29	import org.springframework.context.MessageSourceAware;
    30	import org.springframework.context.support.MessageSourceAccessor;
    31	import org.springframework.core.log.LogMessage;
    32	import org.springframework.security.core.Authentication;
    33	import org.springframework.security.core.AuthenticationException;
    34	import org.springframework.security.core.CredentialsContainer;
    35	import org.springframework.security.core.SpringSecurityMessageSource;
    36	import org.springframework.util.Assert;
    37	import org.springframework.util.CollectionUtils;
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Iterates an {@link Authentication} request through a list of
    41	 * {@link AuthenticationProvider}s.
    42	 *
    43	 * <p>
    44	 * <tt>AuthenticationProvider</tt>s are usually tried in order until one provides a
    45	 * non-null response. A non-null response indicates the provider had authority to decide
    46	 * on the authentication request and no further providers are tried. If a subsequent
    47	 * provider successfully authenticates the request, the earlier authentication exception
    48	 * is disregarded and the successful authentication will be used. If no subsequent
    49	 * provider provides a non-null response, or a new <code>AuthenticationException</code>,
    50	 * the last <code>AuthenticationException</code> received will be used. If no provider
    51	 * returns a non-null response, or indicates it can even process an
    52	 * <code>Authentication</code>, the <code>ProviderManager</code> will throw a
    53	 * <code>ProviderNotFoundException</code>. A parent {@code AuthenticationManager} can also
    54	 * be set, and this will also be tried if none of the configured providers can perform the
    55	 * authentication. This is intended to support namespace configuration options though and
    56	 * is not a feature that should normally be required.
    57	 * <p>
    58	 * The exception to this process is when a provider throws an
    59	 * {@link AccountStatusException}, in which case no further providers in the list will be
    60	 * queried.
    61	 *
    62	 * Post-authentication, the credentials will be cleared from the returned
    63	 * {@code Authentication} object, if it implements the {@link CredentialsContainer}
    64	 * interface. This behaviour can be controlled by modifying the
    65	 * {@link #setEraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication(boolean)
    66	 * eraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication} property.
    67	 *
    68	 * <h2>Event Publishing</h2>
    69	 * <p>
    70	 * Authentication event publishing is delegated to the configured
    71	 * {@link AuthenticationEventPublisher} which defaults to a null implementation which
    72	 * doesn't publish events, so if you are configuring the bean yourself you must inject a
    73	 * publisher bean if you want to receive events. The standard implementation is
    74	 * {@link DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher} which maps common exceptions to events (in
    75	 * the case of authentication failure) and publishes an
    76	 * {@link org.springframework.security.authentication.event.AuthenticationSuccessEvent
    77	 * AuthenticationSuccessEvent} if authentication succeeds. If you are using the namespace
    78	 * then an instance of this bean will be used automatically by the <tt>&lt;http&gt;</tt>
    79	 * configuration, so you will receive events from the web part of your application
    80	 * automatically.
    81	 * <p>
    82	 * Note that the implementation also publishes authentication failure events when it
    83	 * obtains an authentication result (or an exception) from the "parent"
    84	 * {@code AuthenticationManager} if one has been set. So in this situation, the parent
    85	 * should not generally be configured to publish events or there will be duplicates.
    86	 *
    87	 * @author Ben Alex
    88	 * @author Luke Taylor
    89	 * @see DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher
    90	 */
    91	public class ProviderManager implements AuthenticationManager, MessageSourceAware, InitializingBean {
    92	
    93	        private static final Log logger = LogFactory.getLog(ProviderManager.class);
    94	
    95	        private AuthenticationEventPublisher eventPublisher = new NullEventPublisher();
    96	
    97	        private List<AuthenticationProvider> providers = Collections.emptyList();
    98	
    99	        protected MessageSourceAccessor messages = SpringSecurityMessageSource.getAccessor();
   100	
   101	        private @Nullable AuthenticationManager parent;
   102	
   103	        private boolean eraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication = true;
   104	
   105	        /**
   106	         * Construct a {@link ProviderManager} using the given {@link AuthenticationProvider}s
   107	         * @param providers the {@link AuthenticationProvider}s to use
   108	         */
   109	        public ProviderManager(AuthenticationProvider... providers) {
   110	                this(Arrays.asList(providers), null);
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        /**
   114	         * Construct a {@link ProviderManager} using the given {@link AuthenticationProvider}s
   115	         * @param providers the {@link AuthenticationProvider}s to use
   116	         */
   117	        public ProviderManager(List<AuthenticationProvider> providers) {
   118	                this(providers, null);
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        /**
   122	         * Construct a {@link ProviderManager} using the provided parameters
   123	         * @param providers the {@link AuthenticationProvider}s to use
   124	         * @param parent a parent {@link AuthenticationManager} to fall back to
   125	         */
   126	        public ProviderManager(List<AuthenticationProvider> providers, @Nullable AuthenticationManager parent) {
   127	                Assert.notNull(providers, "providers list cannot be null");
   128	                this.providers = providers;
   129	                this.parent = parent;
   130	                checkState();
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        @Override
   134	        public void afterPropertiesSet() {
   135	                checkState();
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        private void checkState() {
   139	                Assert.isTrue(this.parent != null || !this.providers.isEmpty(),
   140	                                "A parent AuthenticationManager or a list of AuthenticationProviders is required");
   141	                Assert.isTrue(!CollectionUtils.contains(this.providers.iterator(), null),
   142	                                "providers list cannot contain null values");
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        /**
   146	         * Attempts to authenticate the passed {@link Authentication} object.
   147	         * <p>
   148	         * The list of {@link AuthenticationProvider}s will be successively tried until an
   149	         * <code>AuthenticationProvider</code> indicates it is capable of authenticating the
   150	         * type of <code>Authentication</code> object passed. Authentication will then be
   151	         * attempted with that <code>AuthenticationProvider</code>.
   152	         * <p>
   153	         * If more than one <code>AuthenticationProvider</code> supports the passed
   154	         * <code>Authentication</code> object, the first one able to successfully authenticate
   155	         * the <code>Authentication</code> object determines the <code>result</code>,
   156	         * overriding any possible <code>AuthenticationException</code> thrown by earlier
   157	         * supporting <code>AuthenticationProvider</code>s. On successful authentication, no
   158	         * subsequent <code>AuthenticationProvider</code>s will be tried. If authentication
   159	         * was not successful by any supporting <code>AuthenticationProvider</code> the last
   160	         * thrown <code>AuthenticationException</code> will be rethrown.
   161	         * @param authentication the authentication request object.
   162	         * @return a fully authenticated object including credentials.
   163	         * @throws AuthenticationException if authentication fails.
   164	         */
   165	        @Override
   166	        public Authentication authenticate(Authentication authentication) throws AuthenticationException {
   167	                Class<? extends Authentication> toTest = authentication.getClass();
   168	                AuthenticationException lastException = null;
   169	                AuthenticationException parentException = null;
   170	                Authentication result = null;
   171	                Authentication parentResult = null;
   172	                int currentPosition = 0;
   173	                int size = this.providers.size();
   174	                for (AuthenticationProvider provider : getProviders()) {
   175	                        if (!provider.supports(toTest)) {
   176	                                continue;
   177	                        }
   178	                        if (logger.isTraceEnabled()) {
   179	                                logger.trace(LogMessage.format("Authenticating request with %s (%d/%d)",
   180	                                                provider.getClass().getSimpleName(), ++currentPosition, size));
   181	                        }
   182	                        try {
   183	                                result = provider.authenticate(authentication);
   184	                                if (result != null) {
   185	                                        copyDetails(authentication, result);
   186	                                        break;
   187	                                }
   188	                        }
   189	                        catch (AccountStatusException ex) {
   190	                                prepareException(ex, authentication);
   191	                                logger.debug(LogMessage.format("Authentication failed for user '%s' since their account status is %s",
   192	                                                authentication.getName(), ex.getMessage()), ex);
   193	                                // SEC-546: Avoid polling additional providers if auth failure is due to
   194	                                // invalid account status
   195	                                throw ex;
   196	                        }
   197	                        catch (InternalAuthenticationServiceException ex) {
   198	                                prepareException(ex, authentication);
   199	                                logger.debug(LogMessage.format("Authentication service failed internally for user '%s'",
   200	                                                authentication.getName()), ex);
   201	                                // SEC-546: Avoid polling additional providers if auth failure is due to
   202	                                // invalid account status
   203	                                throw ex;
   204	                        }
   205	                        catch (AuthenticationException ex) {
   206	                                ex.setAuthenticationRequest(authentication);
   207	                                logger.debug(LogMessage.format("Authentication failed with provider %s since %s",
   208	                                                provider.getClass().getSimpleName(), ex.getMessage()));
   209	                                lastException = ex;
   210	                        }
   211	                }
   212	                if (result == null && this.parent != null) {
   213	                        // Allow the parent to try.
   214	                        try {
   215	                                parentResult = this.parent.authenticate(authentication);
   216	                                result = parentResult;
   217	                        }
   218	                        catch (ProviderNotFoundException ex) {
   219	                                // ignore as we will throw below if no other exception occurred prior to
   220	                                // calling parent and the parent
   221	                                // may throw ProviderNotFound even though a provider in the child already
   222	                                // handled the request
   223	                        }
   224	                        catch (AuthenticationException ex) {
   225	                                parentException = ex;
   226	                                lastException = ex;
   227	                        }
   228	                }
   229	                if (result != null) {
   230	                        if (this.eraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication && (result instanceof CredentialsContainer)) {
   231	                                // Authentication is complete. Remove credentials and other secret data
   232	                                // from authentication
   233	                                ((CredentialsContainer) result).eraseCredentials();
   234	                        }
   235	                        // If the parent AuthenticationManager was attempted and successful then it
   236	                        // will publish an AuthenticationSuccessEvent
   237	                        // This check prevents a duplicate AuthenticationSuccessEvent if the parent
   238	                        // AuthenticationManager already published it
   239	                        if (parentResult == null) {
   240	                                this.eventPublisher.publishAuthenticationSuccess(result);
   241	                        }
   242	
   243	                        return result;
   244	                }
   245	
   246	                // Parent was null, or didn't authenticate (or throw an exception).
   247	                if (lastException == null) {
   248	                        lastException = new ProviderNotFoundException(this.messages.getMessage("ProviderManager.providerNotFound",
   249	                                        new Object[] { toTest.getName() }, "No AuthenticationProvider found for {0}"));
   250	                }
   251	                // If the parent AuthenticationManager was attempted and failed then it will
   252	                // publish an AbstractAuthenticationFailureEvent
   253	                // This check prevents a duplicate AbstractAuthenticationFailureEvent if the
   254	                // parent AuthenticationManager already published it
   255	                if (parentException == null) {
   256	                        prepareException(lastException, authentication);
   257	                }
   258	
   259	                // Ensure this message is not logged when authentication is attempted by
   260	                // the parent provider
   261	                if (this.parent != null) {
   262	                        logger.debug("Denying authentication since all attempted providers failed");
   263	                }
   264	
   265	                throw lastException;
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
   269	        private void prepareException(AuthenticationException ex, Authentication auth) {
   270	                ex.setAuthenticationRequest(auth);
   271	                this.eventPublisher.publishAuthenticationFailure(ex, auth);
   272	        }
   273	
   274	        /**
   275	         * Copies the authentication details from a source Authentication object to a
   276	         * destination one, provided the latter does not already have one set.
   277	         * @param source source authentication
   278	         * @param dest the destination authentication object
   279	         */
   280	        private void copyDetails(Authentication source, Authentication dest) {
   281	                if ((dest instanceof AbstractAuthenticationToken token) && (dest.getDetails() == null)) {
   282	                        token.setDetails(source.getDetails());
   283	                }
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        public List<AuthenticationProvider> getProviders() {
   287	                return this.providers;
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        @Override
   291	        public void setMessageSource(MessageSource messageSource) {
   292	                this.messages = new MessageSourceAccessor(messageSource);
   293	        }
   294	
   295	        public void setAuthenticationEventPublisher(AuthenticationEventPublisher eventPublisher) {
   296	                Assert.notNull(eventPublisher, "AuthenticationEventPublisher cannot be null");
   297	                this.eventPublisher = eventPublisher;
   298	        }
   299	
   300	        /**
   301	         * If set to, a resulting {@code Authentication} which implements the
   302	         * {@code CredentialsContainer} interface will have its
   303	         * {@link CredentialsContainer#eraseCredentials() eraseCredentials} method called
   304	         * before it is returned from the {@code authenticate()} method.
   305	         * @param eraseSecretData set to {@literal false} to retain the credentials data in
   306	         * memory. Defaults to {@literal true}.
   307	         */
   308	        public void setEraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication(boolean eraseSecretData) {
   309	                this.eraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication = eraseSecretData;
   310	        }
   311	
   312	        public boolean isEraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication() {
   313	                return this.eraseCredentialsAfterAuthentication;
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        private static final class NullEventPublisher implements AuthenticationEventPublisher {
   317	
   318	                @Override
   319	                public void publishAuthenticationFailure(AuthenticationException exception, Authentication authentication) {
   320	                }
   321	
   322	                @Override
   323	                public void publishAuthenticationSuccess(Authentication authentication) {
   324	                }
   325	
   326	        }
   327	
   328	}

Now I understand the issue. The `WebAuthnConfigurer` creates a new `ProviderManager` for the `WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter` at line 180:

```java
webAuthnAuthnFilter.setAuthenticationManager(
    new ProviderManager(new WebAuthnAuthenticationProvider(rpOperations, userDetailsService)));
```

But it doesn't set an `AuthenticationEventPublisher` on this `ProviderManager`, so it defaults to `NullEventPublisher`. The global `AuthenticationEventPublisher` is never passed to this `ProviderManager`.
