    71	@Configuration(proxyBeanMethods = false)
    72	class HttpSecurityConfiguration {
    73	
    74	        private static final String BEAN_NAME_PREFIX = "org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.configuration.HttpSecurityConfiguration.";
    75	
    76	        private static final String HTTPSECURITY_BEAN_NAME = BEAN_NAME_PREFIX + "httpSecurity";
    77	
    78	        private ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor;
    79	
    80	        private AuthenticationConfiguration authenticationConfiguration;
    81	
    82	        private ApplicationContext context;
    83	
    84	        private SecurityContextHolderStrategy securityContextHolderStrategy = SecurityContextHolder
    85	                .getContextHolderStrategy();
    86	
    87	        private ContentNegotiationStrategy contentNegotiationStrategy = new HeaderContentNegotiationStrategy();
    88	
    89	        @Autowired
    90	        void setObjectPostProcessor(ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor) {
    91	                this.objectPostProcessor = objectPostProcessor;
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        @Autowired
    95	        void setAuthenticationConfiguration(AuthenticationConfiguration authenticationConfiguration) {
    96	                this.authenticationConfiguration = authenticationConfiguration;
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        @Autowired
   100	        void setApplicationContext(ApplicationContext context) {
   101	                this.context = context;
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        @Autowired(required = false)
   105	        void setSecurityContextHolderStrategy(SecurityContextHolderStrategy securityContextHolderStrategy) {
   106	                this.securityContextHolderStrategy = securityContextHolderStrategy;
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        @Autowired(required = false)
   110	        void setContentNegotiationStrategy(ContentNegotiationStrategy contentNegotiationStrategy) {
   111	                this.contentNegotiationStrategy = contentNegotiationStrategy;
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        @Bean(HTTPSECURITY_BEAN_NAME)
   115	        @Scope("prototype")
   116	        HttpSecurity httpSecurity() {
   117	                LazyPasswordEncoder passwordEncoder = new LazyPasswordEncoder(this.context);
   118	                AuthenticationManagerBuilder authenticationBuilder = new DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder(
   119	                                this.objectPostProcessor, passwordEncoder);
   120	                authenticationBuilder.parentAuthenticationManager(authenticationManager());
   121	                authenticationBuilder.authenticationEventPublisher(getAuthenticationEventPublisher());
   122	                HttpSecurity http = new HttpSecurity(this.objectPostProcessor, authenticationBuilder, createSharedObjects());
   123	                WebAsyncManagerIntegrationFilter webAsyncManagerIntegrationFilter = new WebAsyncManagerIntegrationFilter();
   124	                webAsyncManagerIntegrationFilter.setSecurityContextHolderStrategy(this.securityContextHolderStrategy);
   125	                // @formatter:off
   126	                http
   127	                        .csrf(withDefaults())
   128	                        .addFilter(webAsyncManagerIntegrationFilter)
   129	                        .exceptionHandling(withDefaults())
   130	                        .headers(withDefaults())
   131	                        .sessionManagement(withDefaults())
   132	                        .securityContext(withDefaults())
   133	                        .requestCache(withDefaults())
   134	                        .anonymous(withDefaults())
   135	                        .servletApi(withDefaults())
   136	                        .with(new DefaultLoginPageConfigurer<>());
   137	                http.logout(withDefaults());
   138	                // @formatter:on
   139	                applyCorsIfAvailable(http);
   140	                applyDefaultConfigurers(http);
   141	                applyHttpSecurityCustomizers(this.context, http);
   142	                applyTopLevelCustomizers(this.context, http);
   143	                return http;
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        private void applyCorsIfAvailable(HttpSecurity http) {
   147	                if (this.context.getBeanNamesForType(UrlBasedCorsConfigurationSource.class).length > 0) {
   148	                        http.cors(withDefaults());
   149	                }
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        private AuthenticationManager authenticationManager() {
   153	                return this.authenticationConfiguration.getAuthenticationManager();
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        private AuthenticationEventPublisher getAuthenticationEventPublisher() {
   157	                if (this.context.getBeanNamesForType(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class).length > 0) {
   158	                        return this.context.getBean(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class);
   159	                }
   160	                return this.objectPostProcessor.postProcess(new DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher());
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        private void applyDefaultConfigurers(HttpSecurity http) {
   164	                ClassLoader classLoader = this.context.getClassLoader();
   165	                List<AbstractHttpConfigurer> defaultHttpConfigurers = SpringFactoriesLoader
   166	                        .loadFactories(AbstractHttpConfigurer.class, classLoader);
   167	                for (AbstractHttpConfigurer configurer : defaultHttpConfigurers) {
   168	                        http.with(configurer);
   169	                }
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        /**
   173	         * Applies all {@code Customizer<HttpSecurity>} Bean instances to the
   174	         * {@link HttpSecurity} instance.
   175	         * @param applicationContext the {@link ApplicationContext} to lookup Bean instances
   176	         * @param http the {@link HttpSecurity} to apply the Beans to.
   177	         */
   178	        private void applyHttpSecurityCustomizers(ApplicationContext applicationContext, HttpSecurity http) {
   179	                ResolvableType httpSecurityCustomizerType = ResolvableType.forClassWithGenerics(Customizer.class,
   180	                                HttpSecurity.class);
   181	                ObjectProvider<Customizer<HttpSecurity>> customizerProvider = this.context
   182	                        .getBeanProvider(httpSecurityCustomizerType);
   183	
   184	                // @formatter:off
   185	                customizerProvider.orderedStream().forEach((customizer) ->
   186	                                customizer.customize(http)
   187	                );
   188	                // @formatter:on
   189	        }
   190	
   191	        /**
   192	         * Applies all {@link Customizer} Beans to {@link HttpSecurity}. For each public,
   193	         * non-static method in HttpSecurity that accepts a Customizer
   194	         * <ul>
   195	         * <li>Use the {@link MethodParameter} (this preserves generics) to resolve all Beans
   196	         * for that type</li>
   197	         * <li>For each {@link Customizer} Bean invoke the {@link java.lang.reflect.Method}
   198	         * with the {@link Customizer} Bean as the argument</li>
   199	         * </ul>
   200	         * @param context the {@link ApplicationContext}
   201	         * @param http the {@link HttpSecurity} @
   202	         */
   203	        private void applyTopLevelCustomizers(ApplicationContext context, HttpSecurity http) {
   204	                ReflectionUtils.MethodFilter isCustomizerMethod = (method) -> {
   205	                        if (Modifier.isStatic(method.getModifiers())) {
   206	                                return false;
   207	                        }
   208	                        if (!Modifier.isPublic(method.getModifiers())) {
   209	                                return false;
   210	                        }
   211	                        if (!method.canAccess(http)) {
   212	                                return false;
   213	                        }
   214	                        if (method.getParameterCount() != 1) {
   215	                                return false;
   216	                        }
   217	                        if (method.getParameterTypes()[0] == Customizer.class) {
   218	                                return true;
   219	                        }
   220	                        return false;
   221	                };
   222	                ReflectionUtils.MethodCallback invokeWithEachCustomizerBean = (customizerMethod) -> {
   223	
   224	                        MethodParameter customizerParameter = new MethodParameter(customizerMethod, 0);
   225	                        ResolvableType customizerType = ResolvableType.forMethodParameter(customizerParameter);
   226	                        ObjectProvider<?> customizerProvider = context.getBeanProvider(customizerType);
   227	
   228	                        // @formatter:off
   229	                        customizerProvider.orderedStream().forEach((customizer) ->
   230	                                ReflectionUtils.invokeMethod(customizerMethod, http, customizer)
   231	                        );
   232	                        // @formatter:on
   233	
   234	                };
   235	                ReflectionUtils.doWithMethods(HttpSecurity.class, invokeWithEachCustomizerBean, isCustomizerMethod);
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        private Map<Class<?>, Object> createSharedObjects() {
   239	                Map<Class<?>, Object> sharedObjects = new HashMap<>();
   240	                sharedObjects.put(ApplicationContext.class, this.context);
   241	                sharedObjects.put(ContentNegotiationStrategy.class, this.contentNegotiationStrategy);
   242	                sharedObjects.put(PathPatternRequestMatcher.Builder.class, constructRequestMatcherBuilder(this.context));
   243	                return sharedObjects;
   244	        }
   245	
   246	        private PathPatternRequestMatcher.Builder constructRequestMatcherBuilder(ApplicationContext context) {
   247	                PathPatternRequestMatcherBuilderFactoryBean requestMatcherBuilder = new PathPatternRequestMatcherBuilderFactoryBean();
   248	                requestMatcherBuilder.setApplicationContext(context);
   249	                requestMatcherBuilder.setBeanFactory(context.getAutowireCapableBeanFactory());
   250	                requestMatcherBuilder.setBeanName(requestMatcherBuilder.toString());
   251	                return ThrowingSupplier.of(requestMatcherBuilder::getObject).get();
   252	        }
   253	
   254	        static class DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder extends AuthenticationManagerBuilder {
   255	
   256	                private PasswordEncoder defaultPasswordEncoder;
   257	
   258	                /**
   259	                 * Creates a new instance
   260	                 * @param objectPostProcessor the {@link ObjectPostProcessor} instance to use.
   261	                 */
   262	                DefaultPasswordEncoderAuthenticationManagerBuilder(ObjectPostProcessor<Object> objectPostProcessor,
   263	                                PasswordEncoder defaultPasswordEncoder) {
   264	                        super(objectPostProcessor);
   265	                        this.defaultPasswordEncoder = defaultPasswordEncoder;
   266	                }
   267	
   268	                @Override
   269	                public InMemoryUserDetailsManagerConfigurer<AuthenticationManagerBuilder> inMemoryAuthentication() {
   270	                        return super.inMemoryAuthentication().passwordEncoder(this.defaultPasswordEncoder);
   271	                }
   272	
   273	                @Override
   274	                public JdbcUserDetailsManagerConfigurer<AuthenticationManagerBuilder> jdbcAuthentication() {
   275	                        return super.jdbcAuthentication().passwordEncoder(this.defaultPasswordEncoder);
   276	                }
   277	
   278	                @Override
   279	                public <T extends UserDetailsService> DaoAuthenticationConfigurer<AuthenticationManagerBuilder, T> userDetailsService(
   280	                                T userDetailsService) {
   281	                        return super.userDetailsService(userDetailsService).passwordEncoder(this.defaultPasswordEncoder);
   282	                }
   283	
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        static class LazyPasswordEncoder implements PasswordEncoder {
   287	
   288	                private ApplicationContext applicationContext;
   289	
   290	                private PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder;
   291	
   292	                LazyPasswordEncoder(ApplicationContext applicationContext) {
   293	                        this.applicationContext = applicationContext;
   294	                }
   295	
   296	                @Override
   297	                @Contract("!null -> !null; null -> null")
   298	                public String encode(CharSequence rawPassword) {
   299	                        return getPasswordEncoder().encode(rawPassword);
   300	                }
   301	
   302	                @Override
   303	                public boolean matches(CharSequence rawPassword, String encodedPassword) {
   304	                        return getPasswordEncoder().matches(rawPassword, encodedPassword);
   305	                }
   306	
   307	                @Override
   308	                public boolean upgradeEncoding(String encodedPassword) {
   309	                        return getPasswordEncoder().upgradeEncoding(encodedPassword);
   310	                }
   311	
   312	                private PasswordEncoder getPasswordEncoder() {
   313	                        if (this.passwordEncoder != null) {
   314	                                return this.passwordEncoder;
   315	                        }
   316	                        this.passwordEncoder = this.applicationContext.getBeanProvider(PasswordEncoder.class)
   317	                                .getIfUnique(PasswordEncoderFactories::createDelegatingPasswordEncoder);
   318	                        return this.passwordEncoder;
   319	                }
   320	
   321	                @Override
   322	                public String toString() {
   323	                        return getPasswordEncoder().toString();
   324	                }
   325	
   326	        }

2026-05-30 03:26:10,673 - INFO - swea-agent-spring-projects__spring-security-18938 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the full picture. The `HttpSecurityConfiguration` sets up the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` on the `AuthenticationManagerBuilder`. But the `WebAuthnConfigurer` creates its own `ProviderManager` directly (without going through the builder), so it never gets the `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

The fix should be to retrieve the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` from the application context and set it on the `ProviderManager` created for WebAuthn. Let me look at how the `WebAuthnConfigurer` can get access to it.

Let me look at how to get the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` in the `WebAuthnConfigurer`:

2026-05-30 03:26:17,659 - INFO - swea-agent-spring-projects__spring-security-18938 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear picture. The fix should be in `WebAuthnConfigurer.java` to retrieve the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` from the application context and set it on the `ProviderManager` (or on the `WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter`'s authentication manager).

Let me look at the WebAuthnConfigurer's configure method more carefully. The issue is that a new `ProviderManager` is created for WebAuthn authentication, but it doesn't get the global `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

Now, there are two possible approaches:
1. Set the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` on the `ProviderManager` created for WebAuthn
2. Or, better: the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` on the `ProviderManager` is for publishing events from the `AuthenticationProvider`. But the `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter` (parent of `WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter`) also publishes `InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent` through its own `eventPublisher` (which is `ApplicationEventPublisher`). 

The PR description mentions that `NullEventPublisher` is always used. Looking at line 178-179 in `WebAuthnConfigurer`, the `NullEventPublisher` is the default in `ProviderManager`. The fix should ensure the global `AuthenticationEventPublisher` is set on the `ProviderManager` used for WebAuthn.

Let me check if there is already a shared object or way to get the `AuthenticationEventPublisher`:

2026-05-30 03:26:26,656 - INFO - swea-agent-spring-projects__spring-security-18938 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I see the pattern. Let me look at how `AbstractAuthenticationFilterConfigurer` gets the `AuthenticationManager` - it uses the shared object from `HttpSecurity`:

```java
this.authFilter.setAuthenticationManager(http.getSharedObject(AuthenticationManager.class));
```

The `WebAuthnConfigurer` is different - it creates its own `ProviderManager` rather than using the shared `AuthenticationManager`. This is because WebAuthn needs a different authentication provider.

But the problem is that the `ProviderManager` it creates doesn't have the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` set. Let me now implement the fix.

The simplest and most correct fix is to look up the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` from the application context and set it on the `ProviderManager` created for WebAuthn authentication.

Let me write the fix:

    57	/**
    58	 * Configures WebAuthn for Spring Security applications
    59	 *
    60	 * @param <H> the type of builder
    61	 * @author Rob Winch
    62	 * @since 6.4
    63	 */
    64	public class WebAuthnConfigurer<H extends HttpSecurityBuilder<H>>
    65	                extends AbstractHttpConfigurer<WebAuthnConfigurer<H>, H> {
    66

    68	
    69	        private String rpName;

    79	        /**

    81	         * @param rpId the relying party id
    82	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
    83	         */
    84	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> rpId(String rpId) {
    85	                Assert.hasText(rpId, "rpId be null or empty");
    86	                this.rpId = rpId;
    87	                return this;
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        /**
    91	         * Sets the relying party name

    95	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> rpName(String rpName) {
    96	                Assert.hasText(rpName, "rpName can't be null or empty");
    97	                this.rpName = rpName;
    98	                return this;
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        /**
   102	         * Convenience method for {@link #allowedOrigins(Set)}
   103	         * @param allowedOrigins the allowed origins
   104	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   105	         * @see #allowedOrigins(Set)
   106	         */
   107	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> allowedOrigins(String... allowedOrigins) {
   108	                return allowedOrigins(Set.of(allowedOrigins));
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        /**
   112	         * Sets the allowed origins.
   113	         * @param allowedOrigins the allowed origins

   116	         */
   117	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> allowedOrigins(Set<String> allowedOrigins) {
   118	                Assert.notNull(allowedOrigins, "allowedOrigins can't be null");
   119	                this.allowedOrigins = allowedOrigins;
   120	                return this;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        /**
   124	         * Configures whether the default webauthn registration should be disabled. Setting it
   125	         * to {@code true} will prevent the configurer from registering the
   126	         * {@link DefaultWebAuthnRegistrationPageGeneratingFilter}.
   127	         * @param disable disable the default registration page if true, enable it otherwise
   128	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   129	         */
   130	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> disableDefaultRegistrationPage(boolean disable) {
   131	                this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage = disable;
   132	                return this;
   133	        }
   134

   136	         * Sets {@link HttpMessageConverter} used for WebAuthn to read/write to the HTTP

   141	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> messageConverter(HttpMessageConverter<Object> converter) {
   142	                Assert.notNull(converter, "converter can't be null");
   143	                this.converter = converter;

   152	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> creationOptionsRepository(

   154	                Assert.notNull(creationOptionsRepository, "creationOptionsRepository can't be null");
   155	                this.creationOptionsRepository = creationOptionsRepository;
   156	                return this;

   159	        @Override
   160	        public void init(H http) {
   161	                ExceptionHandlingConfigurer<H> exceptions = http.getConfigurer(ExceptionHandlingConfigurer.class);
   162	                if (exceptions != null) {
   163	                        AuthenticationEntryPoint entryPoint = new LoginUrlAuthenticationEntryPoint("/login");
   164	                        exceptions.defaultDeniedHandlerForMissingAuthority((ep) -> ep.defaultEntryPoint(entryPoint),
   165	                                        FactorGrantedAuthority.WEBAUTHN_AUTHORITY);
   166	                }
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        @Override
   170	        public void configure(H http) {
   171	                UserDetailsService userDetailsService = getSharedOrBean(http, UserDetailsService.class)
   172	                        .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Missing UserDetailsService Bean"));
   173	                PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntities = getSharedOrBean(http,
   174	                                PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository.class)
   175	                        .orElse(userEntityRepository());
   176	                UserCredentialRepository userCredentials = getSharedOrBean(http, UserCredentialRepository.class)
   177	                        .orElse(userCredentialRepository());
   178	                WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations rpOperations = webAuthnRelyingPartyOperations(userEntities, userCredentials);
   179	                PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository = creationOptionsRepository();
   180	                WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter webAuthnAuthnFilter = new WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter();
   181	                ProviderManager providerManager = new ProviderManager(
   182	                                new WebAuthnAuthenticationProvider(rpOperations, userDetailsService));
   183	                providerManager.setAuthenticationEventPublisher(getAuthenticationEventPublisher(http));
   184	                webAuthnAuthnFilter.setAuthenticationManager(providerManager);
   185	                webAuthnAuthnFilter = postProcess(webAuthnAuthnFilter);
   186	                WebAuthnRegistrationFilter webAuthnRegistrationFilter = new WebAuthnRegistrationFilter(userCredentials,
   187	                                rpOperations);
   188	                webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setDeleteCredentialAuthorizationManager(
   189	                                new CredentialRecordOwnerAuthorizationManager(userCredentials, userEntities));
   190	                PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsFilter creationOptionsFilter = new PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsFilter(
   191	                                rpOperations);
   192	                if (creationOptionsRepository != null) {
   193	                        webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);
   194	                        creationOptionsFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);
   195	                }
   196	                if (this.converter != null) {
   197	                        webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   198	                        creationOptionsFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   199	                }
   200	                http.addFilterBefore(webAuthnAuthnFilter, BasicAuthenticationFilter.class);
   201	                http.addFilterAfter(webAuthnRegistrationFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);
   202	                http.addFilterBefore(creationOptionsFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);
   203	                http.addFilterBefore(new PublicKeyCredentialRequestOptionsFilter(rpOperations), AuthorizationFilter.class);
   204	
   205	                DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter loginPageGeneratingFilter = http
   206	                        .getSharedObject(DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter.class);
   207	                boolean isLoginPageEnabled = loginPageGeneratingFilter != null && loginPageGeneratingFilter.isEnabled();
   208	                if (isLoginPageEnabled) {
   209	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setPasskeysEnabled(true);
   210	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setResolveHeaders((request) -> {
   211	                                CsrfToken csrfToken = (CsrfToken) request.getAttribute(CsrfToken.class.getName());
   212	                                return Map.of(csrfToken.getHeaderName(), csrfToken.getToken());
   213	                        });
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                if (!this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage) {
   217	                        http.addFilterAfter(new DefaultWebAuthnRegistrationPageGeneratingFilter(userEntities, userCredentials),
   218	                                        AuthorizationFilter.class);
   219	                        if (!isLoginPageEnabled) {
   220	                                http.addFilter(DefaultResourcesFilter.css());
   221	                        }
   222	                }
   223	
   224	                if (isLoginPageEnabled || !this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage) {
   225	                        http.addFilter(DefaultResourcesFilter.webauthn());
   226	                }
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        private PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository() {
   230	                if (this.creationOptionsRepository != null) {
   231	                        return this.creationOptionsRepository;
   232	                }
   233	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   234	                return context.getBeanProvider(PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository.class).getIfUnique();
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        private <C> Optional<C> getSharedOrBean(H http, Class<C> type) {
   238	                C shared = http.getSharedObject(type);
   239	                return Optional.ofNullable(shared).or(() -> getBeanOrNull(type));
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        private <T> Optional<T> getBeanOrNull(Class<T> type) {
   243	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   244	                if (context == null) {
   245	                        return Optional.empty();
   246	                }
   247	                try {
   248	                        return Optional.of(context.getBean(type));
   249	                }
   250	                catch (NoSuchBeanDefinitionException ex) {
   251	                        return Optional.empty();
   252	                }
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        private MapUserCredentialRepository userCredentialRepository() {
   256	                return new MapUserCredentialRepository();
   257	        }

   260	                return new MapPublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository();
   261	        }

   265	                Optional<WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations> webauthnOperationsBean = getBeanOrNull(
   266	                                WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations.class);
   267	                String rpName = (this.rpName != null) ? this.rpName : this.rpId;
   268	                return webauthnOperationsBean
   269	                        .orElseGet(() -> new Webauthn4JRelyingPartyOperations(userEntities, userCredentials,
   270	                                        PublicKeyCredentialRpEntity.builder().id(this.rpId).name(rpName).build(), this.allowedOrigins));
   271	        }

   273	        private AuthenticationEventPublisher getAuthenticationEventPublisher(H http) {
   274	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   275	                if (context.getBeanNamesForType(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class).length > 0) {
   276	                        return context.getBean(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class);
   277	                }
   278	                return new DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher();
   279	        }

   132	        public void webauthnWhenFormLoginAndDefaultRegistrationPageConfiguredThenNoDuplicateFilters() {
   133	                this.spring.register(DefaultWebauthnConfiguration.class).autowire();
   134	                FilterChainProxy filterChain = this.spring.getContext().getBean(FilterChainProxy.class);
   135	
   136	                List<DefaultResourcesFilter> defaultResourcesFilters = filterChain.getFilterChains()
   137	                        .get(0)
   138	                        .getFilters()
   139	                        .stream()
   140	                        .filter(DefaultResourcesFilter.class::isInstance)
   141	                        .map(DefaultResourcesFilter.class::cast)
   142	                        .toList();
   143	
   144	                assertThat(defaultResourcesFilters).map(DefaultResourcesFilter::toString)
   145	                        .filteredOn((filterDescription) -> filterDescription.contains("login/webauthn.js"))
   146	                        .hasSize(1);
   147	                assertThat(defaultResourcesFilters).map(DefaultResourcesFilter::toString)
   148	                        .filteredOn((filterDescription) -> filterDescription.contains("default-ui.css"))
   149	                        .hasSize(1);
   150	        }

   288	        static class ConfigCredentialCreationOptionsRepository {
   289

   291

1. I added imports for `AuthenticationEventPublisher` and `DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher`.

3. I added a `getAuthenticationEventPublisher` method that mimics the pattern used in `HttpSecurityConfiguration.getAuthenticationEventPublisher()`:

The method:
- Gets the `ApplicationContext` from shared objects
- If there's a bean of type `AuthenticationEventPublisher` in the context, it uses that (this is the global configured one)
- Otherwise it creates a `DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher`

This matches the pattern used in `HttpSecurityConfiguration.getAuthenticationEventPublisher()` (lines 156-161) and `AuthenticationConfiguration.getAuthenticationEventPublisher()` (lines 146-151).

However, I notice that in both `HttpSecurityConfiguration` and `AuthenticationConfiguration`, the `DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher` is post-processed via `objectPostProcessor.postProcess(new DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher())`. Let me check if I should do the same.

Looking at the code in `WebAuthnConfigurer`, it extends `AbstractHttpConfigurer` which has access to `postProcess` (as seen on line 185: `webAuthnAuthnFilter = postProcess(webAuthnAuthnFilter)`). However, the `getAuthenticationEventPublisher` method doesn't have easy access to `postProcess` and the pattern in `HttpSecurityConfiguration` uses an injected `objectPostProcessor`.

    19	import org.springframework.context.ApplicationContext;
    20	import org.springframework.security.config.ObjectPostProcessor;
    21	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.SecurityConfigurer;
    22	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.SecurityConfigurerAdapter;
    23	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.HttpSecurityBuilder;
    24	import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.builders.HttpSecurity;
    25	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolder;
    26	import org.springframework.security.core.context.SecurityContextHolderStrategy;
    27	import org.springframework.security.web.DefaultSecurityFilterChain;
    28	import org.springframework.security.web.servlet.util.matcher.PathPatternRequestMatcher;
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * Adds a convenient base class for {@link SecurityConfigurer} instances that operate on
    32	 * {@link HttpSecurity}.
    33	 *
    34	 * @author Rob Winch
    35	 * @author Ding Hao
    36	 */
    37	public abstract class AbstractHttpConfigurer<T extends AbstractHttpConfigurer<T, B>, B extends HttpSecurityBuilder<B>>
    38	                extends SecurityConfigurerAdapter<DefaultSecurityFilterChain, B> {
    39	
    40	        private SecurityContextHolderStrategy securityContextHolderStrategy;
    41	
    42	        /**
    43	         * Disables the {@link AbstractHttpConfigurer} by removing it. After doing so a fresh
    44	         * version of the configuration can be applied.
    45	         * @return the {@link HttpSecurityBuilder} for additional customizations
    46	         */
    47	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    48	        public B disable() {
    49	                getBuilder().removeConfigurer(getClass());
    50	                return getBuilder();
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    54	        public T withObjectPostProcessor(ObjectPostProcessor<?> objectPostProcessor) {
    55	                addObjectPostProcessor(objectPostProcessor);
    56	                return (T) this;
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        protected SecurityContextHolderStrategy getSecurityContextHolderStrategy() {
    60	                if (this.securityContextHolderStrategy != null) {
    61	                        return this.securityContextHolderStrategy;
    62	                }
    63	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
    64	                this.securityContextHolderStrategy = context.getBeanProvider(SecurityContextHolderStrategy.class)
    65	                        .getIfUnique(SecurityContextHolder::getContextHolderStrategy);
    66	                return this.securityContextHolderStrategy;
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        protected PathPatternRequestMatcher.Builder getRequestMatcherBuilder() {
    70	                return getBuilder().getSharedObject(PathPatternRequestMatcher.Builder.class);
    71	        }
    72	
    73	}

    57	/**
    58	 * Configures WebAuthn for Spring Security applications
    59	 *
    60	 * @param <H> the type of builder
    61	 * @author Rob Winch
    62	 * @since 6.4
    63	 */
    64	public class WebAuthnConfigurer<H extends HttpSecurityBuilder<H>>
    65	                extends AbstractHttpConfigurer<WebAuthnConfigurer<H>, H> {
    66	
    67	        private String rpId;
    68	
    69	        private String rpName;
    70	
    71	        private Set<String> allowedOrigins = new HashSet<>();
    72	
    73	        private boolean disableDefaultRegistrationPage = false;
    74	
    75	        private PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository;
    76	
    77	        private HttpMessageConverter<Object> converter;
    78	
    79	        /**
    80	         * The Relying Party id.
    81	         * @param rpId the relying party id
    82	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
    83	         */
    84	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> rpId(String rpId) {
    85	                Assert.hasText(rpId, "rpId be null or empty");
    86	                this.rpId = rpId;
    87	                return this;
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        /**
    91	         * Sets the relying party name
    92	         * @param rpName the relying party name
    93	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
    94	         */
    95	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> rpName(String rpName) {
    96	                Assert.hasText(rpName, "rpName can't be null or empty");
    97	                this.rpName = rpName;
    98	                return this;
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        /**
   102	         * Convenience method for {@link #allowedOrigins(Set)}
   103	         * @param allowedOrigins the allowed origins
   104	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   105	         * @see #allowedOrigins(Set)
   106	         */
   107	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> allowedOrigins(String... allowedOrigins) {
   108	                return allowedOrigins(Set.of(allowedOrigins));
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        /**
   112	         * Sets the allowed origins.
   113	         * @param allowedOrigins the allowed origins
   114	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   115	         * @see #allowedOrigins(String...)
   116	         */
   117	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> allowedOrigins(Set<String> allowedOrigins) {
   118	                Assert.notNull(allowedOrigins, "allowedOrigins can't be null");
   119	                this.allowedOrigins = allowedOrigins;
   120	                return this;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        /**
   124	         * Configures whether the default webauthn registration should be disabled. Setting it
   125	         * to {@code true} will prevent the configurer from registering the
   126	         * {@link DefaultWebAuthnRegistrationPageGeneratingFilter}.
   127	         * @param disable disable the default registration page if true, enable it otherwise
   128	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   129	         */
   130	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> disableDefaultRegistrationPage(boolean disable) {
   131	                this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage = disable;
   132	                return this;
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        /**
   136	         * Sets {@link HttpMessageConverter} used for WebAuthn to read/write to the HTTP
   137	         * request/response.
   138	         * @param converter the {@link HttpMessageConverter}
   139	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   140	         */
   141	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> messageConverter(HttpMessageConverter<Object> converter) {
   142	                Assert.notNull(converter, "converter can't be null");
   143	                this.converter = converter;
   144	                return this;
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        /**
   148	         * Sets PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository
   149	         * @param creationOptionsRepository the creationOptionsRepository
   150	         * @return the {@link WebAuthnConfigurer} for further customization
   151	         */
   152	        public WebAuthnConfigurer<H> creationOptionsRepository(
   153	                        PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository) {
   154	                Assert.notNull(creationOptionsRepository, "creationOptionsRepository can't be null");
   155	                this.creationOptionsRepository = creationOptionsRepository;
   156	                return this;
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        @Override
   160	        public void init(H http) {
   161	                ExceptionHandlingConfigurer<H> exceptions = http.getConfigurer(ExceptionHandlingConfigurer.class);
   162	                if (exceptions != null) {
   163	                        AuthenticationEntryPoint entryPoint = new LoginUrlAuthenticationEntryPoint("/login");
   164	                        exceptions.defaultDeniedHandlerForMissingAuthority((ep) -> ep.defaultEntryPoint(entryPoint),
   165	                                        FactorGrantedAuthority.WEBAUTHN_AUTHORITY);
   166	                }
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        @Override
   170	        public void configure(H http) {
   171	                UserDetailsService userDetailsService = getSharedOrBean(http, UserDetailsService.class)
   172	                        .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Missing UserDetailsService Bean"));
   173	                PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntities = getSharedOrBean(http,
   174	                                PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository.class)
   175	                        .orElse(userEntityRepository());
   176	                UserCredentialRepository userCredentials = getSharedOrBean(http, UserCredentialRepository.class)
   177	                        .orElse(userCredentialRepository());
   178	                WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations rpOperations = webAuthnRelyingPartyOperations(userEntities, userCredentials);
   179	                PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository = creationOptionsRepository();
   180	                WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter webAuthnAuthnFilter = new WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter();
   181	                ProviderManager providerManager = new ProviderManager(
   182	                                new WebAuthnAuthenticationProvider(rpOperations, userDetailsService));
   183	                providerManager.setAuthenticationEventPublisher(getAuthenticationEventPublisher(http));
   184	                webAuthnAuthnFilter.setAuthenticationManager(providerManager);
   185	                webAuthnAuthnFilter = postProcess(webAuthnAuthnFilter);
   186	                WebAuthnRegistrationFilter webAuthnRegistrationFilter = new WebAuthnRegistrationFilter(userCredentials,
   187	                                rpOperations);
   188	                webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setDeleteCredentialAuthorizationManager(
   189	                                new CredentialRecordOwnerAuthorizationManager(userCredentials, userEntities));
   190	                PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsFilter creationOptionsFilter = new PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsFilter(
   191	                                rpOperations);
   192	                if (creationOptionsRepository != null) {
   193	                        webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);
   194	                        creationOptionsFilter.setCreationOptionsRepository(creationOptionsRepository);
   195	                }
   196	                if (this.converter != null) {
   197	                        webAuthnRegistrationFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   198	                        creationOptionsFilter.setConverter(this.converter);
   199	                }
   200	                http.addFilterBefore(webAuthnAuthnFilter, BasicAuthenticationFilter.class);
   201	                http.addFilterAfter(webAuthnRegistrationFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);
   202	                http.addFilterBefore(creationOptionsFilter, AuthorizationFilter.class);
   203	                http.addFilterBefore(new PublicKeyCredentialRequestOptionsFilter(rpOperations), AuthorizationFilter.class);
   204	
   205	                DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter loginPageGeneratingFilter = http
   206	                        .getSharedObject(DefaultLoginPageGeneratingFilter.class);
   207	                boolean isLoginPageEnabled = loginPageGeneratingFilter != null && loginPageGeneratingFilter.isEnabled();
   208	                if (isLoginPageEnabled) {
   209	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setPasskeysEnabled(true);
   210	                        loginPageGeneratingFilter.setResolveHeaders((request) -> {
   211	                                CsrfToken csrfToken = (CsrfToken) request.getAttribute(CsrfToken.class.getName());
   212	                                return Map.of(csrfToken.getHeaderName(), csrfToken.getToken());
   213	                        });
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                if (!this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage) {
   217	                        http.addFilterAfter(new DefaultWebAuthnRegistrationPageGeneratingFilter(userEntities, userCredentials),
   218	                                        AuthorizationFilter.class);
   219	                        if (!isLoginPageEnabled) {
   220	                                http.addFilter(DefaultResourcesFilter.css());
   221	                        }
   222	                }
   223	
   224	                if (isLoginPageEnabled || !this.disableDefaultRegistrationPage) {
   225	                        http.addFilter(DefaultResourcesFilter.webauthn());
   226	                }
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        private PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository creationOptionsRepository() {
   230	                if (this.creationOptionsRepository != null) {
   231	                        return this.creationOptionsRepository;
   232	                }
   233	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   234	                return context.getBeanProvider(PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsRepository.class).getIfUnique();
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        private <C> Optional<C> getSharedOrBean(H http, Class<C> type) {
   238	                C shared = http.getSharedObject(type);
   239	                return Optional.ofNullable(shared).or(() -> getBeanOrNull(type));
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        private <T> Optional<T> getBeanOrNull(Class<T> type) {
   243	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   244	                if (context == null) {
   245	                        return Optional.empty();
   246	                }
   247	                try {
   248	                        return Optional.of(context.getBean(type));
   249	                }
   250	                catch (NoSuchBeanDefinitionException ex) {
   251	                        return Optional.empty();
   252	                }
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        private MapUserCredentialRepository userCredentialRepository() {
   256	                return new MapUserCredentialRepository();
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        private PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntityRepository() {
   260	                return new MapPublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository();
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        private WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations webAuthnRelyingPartyOperations(
   264	                        PublicKeyCredentialUserEntityRepository userEntities, UserCredentialRepository userCredentials) {
   265	                Optional<WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations> webauthnOperationsBean = getBeanOrNull(
   266	                                WebAuthnRelyingPartyOperations.class);
   267	                String rpName = (this.rpName != null) ? this.rpName : this.rpId;
   268	                return webauthnOperationsBean
   269	                        .orElseGet(() -> new Webauthn4JRelyingPartyOperations(userEntities, userCredentials,
   270	                                        PublicKeyCredentialRpEntity.builder().id(this.rpId).name(rpName).build(), this.allowedOrigins));
   271	        }
   272	
   273	        private AuthenticationEventPublisher getAuthenticationEventPublisher(H http) {
   274	                ApplicationContext context = getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class);
   275	                if (context.getBeanNamesForType(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class).length > 0) {
   276	                        return context.getBean(AuthenticationEventPublisher.class);
   277	                }
   278	                return postProcess(new DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher());
   279	        }

Let me now think about edge cases:\n\n1. **No `ApplicationContext` available**: If `context` is null, `context.getBeanNamesForType(...)` would throw a NPE. However, in normal Spring Security configuration, the `ApplicationContext` should always be available as a shared object. Looking at `HttpSecurityConfiguration.createSharedObjects()`, it always sets the `ApplicationContext`. Also, the existing code in the class already uses `getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class)` in several places without null checks (lines 229, 239, 243), so this pattern is consistent.\n\n2. **`AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean defined**: If a user defines a custom `AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean, it will be picked up and used. This matches the expected behavior described in the PR.\n\n3. **No `AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean defined**: A `DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher` is created and post-processed, which matches the behavior of `HttpSecurityConfiguration` and `AuthenticationConfiguration`.\n\n4. **The `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter` (parent of `WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter`)**: This also has its own `eventPublisher` field (ApplicationEventPublisher) for publishing `InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent`. But that's a separate concern from the `ProviderManager`'s `AuthenticationEventPublisher`. The PR description mentions both `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` (from `ProviderManager`) and the `NullEventPublisher` (the default in `ProviderManager`). The fix addresses the `ProviderManager` issue.\n\nWait, let me re-read the PR description more carefully:\n\n> WebAuthn should use the configured (global) `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.\n\nThe PR mentions that for username/password authentication, `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` is published on the configured `AuthenticationEventPublisher`, but for passkey authentication, it's published on a `NullEventPublisher` (and swallowed).\n\nThe `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` is published by `ProviderManager.publishAuthenticationSuccess()` via `AuthenticationEventPublisher`. The fix I made ensures that the `ProviderManager` used for WebAuthn gets the configured `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.\n\nThis should resolve the issue.\n\nLet me also check if there's also an `InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent` being published by `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter` that might need fixing. Looking at the code:\n\nIn `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter`:\n```java\nif (this.eventPublisher != null) {\n    this.eventPublisher.publishEvent(new InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent(authResult, this.getClass()));\n}\n```\n\nThe `eventPublisher` here is `ApplicationEventPublisher` (set via `setApplicationEventPublisher`). 2026-05-30 03:34:06,610 - INFO - swea-agent-spring-projects__spring-security-18938 - 💭 THOUGHT
The implementation looks correct. Let me now think about edge cases:

1. **No `ApplicationContext` available**: If `context` is null, `context.getBeanNamesForType(...)` would throw a NPE. However, in normal Spring Security configuration, the `ApplicationContext` should always be available as a shared object. Looking at `HttpSecurityConfiguration.createSharedObjects()`, it always sets the `ApplicationContext`. Also, the existing code in the class already uses `getBuilder().getSharedObject(ApplicationContext.class)` in several places without null checks (lines 229, 239, 243), so this pattern is consistent.

2. **`AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean defined**: If a user defines a custom `AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean, it will be picked up and used. This matches the expected behavior described in the PR.

3. **No `AuthenticationEventPublisher` bean defined**: A `DefaultAuthenticationEventPublisher` is created and post-processed, which matches the behavior of `HttpSecurityConfiguration` and `AuthenticationConfiguration`.

4. **The `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter` (parent of `WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter`)**: This also has its own `eventPublisher` field (ApplicationEventPublisher) for publishing `InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent`. But that's a separate concern from the `ProviderManager`'s `AuthenticationEventPublisher`. The PR description mentions both `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` (from `ProviderManager`) and the `NullEventPublisher` (the default in `ProviderManager`). The fix addresses the `ProviderManager` issue.

Wait, let me re-read the PR description more carefully:

> WebAuthn should use the configured (global) `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

The PR mentions that for username/password authentication, `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` is published on the configured `AuthenticationEventPublisher`, but for passkey authentication, it's published on a `NullEventPublisher` (and swallowed).

The `AuthenticationSuccessEvent` is published by `ProviderManager.publishAuthenticationSuccess()` via `AuthenticationEventPublisher`. The fix I made ensures that the `ProviderManager` used for WebAuthn gets the configured `AuthenticationEventPublisher`.

This should resolve the issue.

Let me also check if there's also an `InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent` being published by `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter` that might need fixing. Looking at the code:

In `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter`:
```java
if (this.eventPublisher != null) {
    this.eventPublisher.publishEvent(new InteractiveAuthenticationSuccessEvent(authResult, this.getClass()));
}
```

The `eventPublisher` here is `ApplicationEventPublisher` (set via `setApplicationEventPublisher`). Since `WebAuthnAuthenticationFilter` extends `AbstractAuthenticationProcessingFilter` and is post-processed via `postProcess(webAuthnAuthnFilter)`, the `ApplicationEventPublisher` should be set through the Spring Bean post-processing (since it implements `ApplicationEventPublisherAware`). So that should work fine.

But the PR specifically mentions `NullEventPublisher` which is in `ProviderManager` (line 95-96 of `ProviderManager.java`):
```java
private AuthenticationEventPublisher eventPublisher = new NullEventPublisher();
```

And line 240:
```java
this.eventPublisher.publishAuthenticationSuccess(result);
```

So my fix directly addresses this: I'm setting the `AuthenticationEventPublisher` on the `ProviderManager` used for WebAuthn authentication, so it will use the configured global publisher instead of `NullEventPublisher`.

I believe the fix is complete and correct. Let me run a broader set of tests to ensure nothing is broken:
